Introduction
========================================================================================

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/introduction#overview-of-the-api)

Overview of the API
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Fireflies API is built on top of GraphQL, a powerful interface designed to provide you with efficient and flexible access to your data. This API allows you to retrieve exactly the data you need in a structured format. Whether you are building a web application, a mobile app, or a complex software system, our API caters to a wide range of data requirements. Our API covers various functionalities, including queries for fetching data as well as uploading meeting audio. It is designed to be intuitive and easy to use, ensuring that you can start fetching and manipulating data with minimal setup.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/introduction#advantages-of-using-graphql)

Advantages of Using GraphQL
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Precise Data Fetching:** One of the key strengths of GraphQL is its ability to return exactly what you request and nothing more. This precision eliminates the over-fetching of data, common in traditional REST APIs, leading to more efficient network utilization and faster response times. **2\. Single Endpoint:** Unlike REST APIs, which often require multiple endpoints for different data needs, GraphQL operates through a single endpoint. This simplification streamlines interactions with the API and makes maintaining and managing the API more straightforward. **3\. Flexibility and Scalability:** GraphQL APIs are incredibly flexible, allowing for queries that can evolve with your needs. This flexibility, combined with efficient data retrieval, makes GraphQL an ideal choice for both small projects and large-scale applications. In the following sections, we will guide you through the essential components of our API, provide detailed examples, and offer best practices to help you make the most of our API. Whether you’re a new user or an experienced developer, this documentation is designed to assist you in seamlessly integrating the API into your applications.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/introduction#additional-resources)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the Fireflies.ai Documentation, your essential guide to unlocking the full potential of our API. We understand that diving into a new API can be daunting, and finding the specific information you need shouldn’t add to that challenge. That’s why we’ve designed our documentation to be both comprehensive and user-friendly, ensuring you get the answers you need without the hassle.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/ask-docs#explore-with-fireflies-ai-assistant)

Explore with Fireflies AI Assistant
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With our AI assistant, navigating the documentation becomes as intuitive as having a conversation. Whether you’re looking for detailed API endpoints, integration guides, or troubleshooting tips, our integrated AI assistant is here to assist you every step of the way.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/ask-docs#how-to-use-fireflies-ai-assistant)

How to Use Fireflies AI Assistant

Getting started is simple:

1.  **Access the Search Bar:** Click on the search bar at the top of the page, or use the shortcut `CMD + K` (for Mac users) or `Ctrl + K` (for Windows and Linux users) to jump straight to it.
2.  **Ask Your Question:** Type in your question just as you would when talking to ChatGPT. Whether it’s a broad query about API capabilities or a specific request for code examples, the AI Assistant is ready to provide you with precise answers.

On this page

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the Fireflies.ai Developer Program! This exclusive program offers developers a chance to explore, test, and integrate with our APIs for a limited period of three months. This program is tailored for developers eager to create seamless integrations and unlock the full capabilities of Fireflies.ai. Participants will gain access to premium features and higher rate limits, ensuring a swift and successful project development.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#program-benefits)

Program Benefits
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As a member of the Fireflies.ai Developer Program, you’ll enjoy:

*   **Full Business Tier Access**: Complimentary access to all Business Tier features, tools, and resources
*   **Integration Support**: Get guidance on how to connect the API seamlessly with your application
*   **Enhanced API Access**: Enjoy expanded rate limits and access to premium features designed for high-demand integrations
*   **Community and Updates**: Be part of our developer community and receive the latest updates, tutorials, and API news

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#how-to-apply)

How to Apply
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Interested in joining? Follow these simple steps to apply for the program:

1.  **Fill Out the Application Form**: [Apply here](https://fireflies-developer.paperform.co/)
    
2.  **Verification**: Once you submit the form, our team will review your application. Please note that this process is manual and may take a few business days
3.  **Approval Notification**: If your application is approved, you’ll receive a confirmation email with details about your program access

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#application-requirements)

Application Requirements
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To qualify for the Developer Program, please ensure you have:

*   **A clear project plan**: Briefly describe how Fireflies.ai will integrate with your application
*   **A company email**: A company email is preferred for verification purposes
*   **GitHub Repository**: Optionally, include a GitHub link to your code or previous work to help us understand your technical expertise
*   **Additional Comments**: Any additional information that can help us assess your project’s alignment with our platform goals

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#program-terms)

Program Terms
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Duration**: The complimentary Business Tier access lasts for three months from the date of approval
*   **Feedback**: We may reach out for feedback to better understand your experience and how we can enhance our API

We look forward to seeing what you’ll build and are excited to support your development journey!

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/developer-program#additional-resources)

# MCP Server Configuration - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Getting Started

MCP Server Configuration

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#overview)
    
*   [What is MCP?](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#what-is-mcp%3F)
    
*   [Getting Started](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#getting-started)
    
*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#prerequisites)
    
*   [Installation](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#installation)
    
*   [Use Cases](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#use-cases)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#additional-resources)
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#overview)

Overview

The Fireflies MCP Server enables AI tools to connect directly to your meeting data without switching platforms or copying transcript excerpts. This integration allows you to ask questions like “What were the main objections in this week’s sales calls?” or “Create a summary of all product feedback from user interviews this month” directly from your AI coding tools.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#what-is-mcp%3F)

What is MCP?

Model Context Protocol (MCP) is an open standard that enables AI applications to securely connect to external data sources and tools. With Fireflies MCP Server, your AI tools can access meeting transcripts, summaries, action items, and insights directly from your Fireflies account.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#getting-started)

Getting Started

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   Active Fireflies.ai account
*   AI tool that supports MCP (such as Claude, OpenAI Connector, Cursor, Devin, or other MCP-compatible applications)

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#installation)

Installation

1.  **Configure your AI tool** Add the Fireflies MCP server to your AI tool’s configuration. The remote server URL is [https://api.fireflies.ai/mcp](https://api.fireflies.ai/mcp)
     which uses OAuth with your Fireflies account. The exact steps depend on your specific AI application. For specific AI tools, you can also configure directly through:
    *   [Claude Settings](https://claude.ai/settings/connectors)
        
    *   [Devin MCP Marketplace](https://app.devin.ai/settings/mcp-marketplace/setup/fireflies)
        
2.  **Use your Fireflies API key on Claude Desktop** (Optional):
    1.  Add this config to your `claude_desktop_config.json` file:
        
        Copy
        
        Ask AI
        
            {
              "mcpServers": {
                "fireflies": {
                  "command": "npx",
                  "args": [\
                    "mcp-remote",\
                    "https://api.fireflies.ai/mcp",\
                    "--header",\
                    "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"\
                  ]
                }
              }
            }
            
        
    2.  Get your API Key from Fireflies
        *   Go to **Settings > Developer Settings** and **Copy your API key**
        *   [See how to get your API key →](https://guide.fireflies.ai/hc/en-us/articles/360020249198-How-to-access-the-Fireflies-API-key)
            
        *   Once you have the API key, paste it in your claude\_desktop\_config.json
        *   Replace `YOUR_API_KEY_HERE` with your actual API key
    3.  Restart Claude Desktop
3.  **Start querying your data** Once configured, you can ask your AI tool questions about your meeting data directly.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#use-cases)

Use Cases

*   **Sales Analysis**: “What were the common objections in this week’s sales calls?”
*   **Product Feedback**: “Summarize all product feedback from user interviews this month”
*   **Meeting Insights**: “What action items were assigned to John across all meetings?”
*   **Trend Analysis**: “How has customer sentiment changed over the past quarter?”

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration#additional-resources)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section serves as a primer on the essential features of the Fireflies API. It covers the requirements to make authenticated requests to the Fireflies API, key GraphQL concepts and a breakdown of core components like queries, mutations, schema and data types.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#host)

Host

The Fireflies API is hosted at [https://api.fireflies.ai](https://api.fireflies.ai/)

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#authorization)

Authorization

The Fireflies API requires a valid API key for all requests. Please see [Authorization](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)
 for more information

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#graphql-api-concepts)

GraphQL API Concepts
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to our GraphQL API! GraphQL is a powerful query language designed for APIs, offering clients the ability to request exactly what they need and nothing more.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#queries)

Queries

Queries are used to fetch data in GraphQL. They are akin to the `GET` request in REST. A basic query might look like this:

Queries are read-only and won’t modify your data.

graphql

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
      user(id: "1") {
        name
        email
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#mutations)

Mutations

Mutations allow you to modify data – create, update, or delete.

Mutations should be used with caution as they change server-side data.

graphql

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation {
      setUserRole(user_id: "1", role: "user") {
        id
        name
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#schema-and-types)

Schema and Types
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#schema-definition)

Schema Definition

The schema defines the API’s capabilities, including types, queries, mutations, and more.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#understanding-graphql-schema)

Understanding GraphQL Schema

The schema is a contract between client and server, defining how clients can access data.

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#data-types)

Data Types

**Standard Types:** Int, Float, String, Boolean, ID. **Custom Types:** Defining complex data structures. Custom types are user-defined and can include combinations of standard types.

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#best-practices)

Best Practices

1.  Optimize query performance by requesting for only necessary data.
2.  Use variables in queries to enhance readability and flexibility

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/concepts#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For more in-depth information, visit [GraphQL Documentation](https://graphql.org/learn/)
.

[Quickstart\
----------\
\
Make your first request in under 5 minutes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart)
[Introspection\
-------------\
\
Query generation and API exploration](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Navigation

Getting Started

LLM-based Development

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#overview)
    
*   [How to Use llms.txt Files](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#how-to-use-llms-txt-files)
    
*   [For Tools with Limited Agentic Capabilities](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#for-tools-with-limited-agentic-capabilities)
    
*   [For Advanced, Agentic Coding Tools](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#for-advanced%2C-agentic-coding-tools)
    
*   [Additional Tips](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#additional-tips)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#additional-resources)
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#overview)

Overview

Welcome to the guide on utilizing our specialized `llms.txt` files to enhance your LLM-based coding workflow. Whether you’re using Replit, Cursor, Devin, or any other AI coding tool, this page will assist you in leveraging our resources to debug and refine code generated by Fireflies. Our platform seamlessly integrates with a variety of AI coding tools. While the generated code may not always be perfect, this guide outlines how to effectively use our `llms.txt` files to improve the debugging process, ensuring your development workflow remains smooth and efficient.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#how-to-use-llms-txt-files)

How to Use `llms.txt` Files

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#for-tools-with-limited-agentic-capabilities)

For Tools with Limited Agentic Capabilities

If your coding tool does not support web querying or autonomous resource fetching:

*   **Download the File**  
    Access the complete file by visiting [this link](https://docs.fireflies.ai/llms-full.txt)
     and download it to your local machine.
*   **Upload and Debug**  
    Upload the downloaded file to your AI coding tool. Instruct your tool to analyze and debug the code using the content of this file. This manual intervention guides the tool in identifying and fixing errors in generated code.

#### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#for-advanced%2C-agentic-coding-tools)

For Advanced, Agentic Coding Tools

If your coding tool is sophisticated and capable of querying the web independently:

*   **Provide the URL Directly**  
    Instead of downloading the full file, supply your tool with the URL [https://docs.fireflies.ai/llms-full.txt](https://docs.fireflies.ai/llms-full.txt)
    .
*   **Let It Decide**  
    Your advanced tool will automatically determine which parts of the file to use and where to look, streamlining the debugging process without additional manual steps.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#additional-tips)

Additional Tips

*   **Tool Configuration:** Ensure that your AI coding tool is configured to handle file uploads or URL-based inputs effectively.
*   **Experiment and Adapt:** Different tools may interact with our resources in unique ways. Experiment with both methods to find the approach that best suits your workflow.
*   **Support and Documentation:** If you encounter any challenges or need further assistance, please contact our support team.

Happy coding!

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/llm-development#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Connect your AI tools directly to your meeting data](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/mcp-configuration)

--------\

Fundamentals

Limits

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#overview)

*   [API Rate Limits](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#api-rate-limits)
    
*   [Add to Live API Rate Limit](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#add-to-live-api-rate-limit)
    
*   [Navigating API Rate Limits](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#navigating-api-rate-limits)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Understanding the limitations of our API is crucial for efficient and uninterrupted usage. Below you’ll find detailed information about the upload limits for different file types and the rate limits applicable to various subscription plans.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#upload-limits)

Upload Limits
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Fireflies API accommodates a range of file sizes for different user types. Here’s a breakdown of the maximum file sizes for audio and video uploads:

| Upload Type | Free User Limit | Pro / Business / Enterprise Limit |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Audio Files | Up to 200MB | Up to 200MB |
| Video Files | Up to 100MB | Up to 1.5GB |

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#understanding-upload-limits)

Understanding Upload Limits

*   **Audio Files:** All users can upload an audio file no greater than 200MB, ensuring ample capacity for high-quality audio content.
*   **Video Files for Free Users:** Free users have a maximum upload limit of 100MB for video files, suitable for short clips and previews.
*   **Video Files for Pro/Business/Enterprise Users:** Higher-tier users can upload larger video files up to 1.5GB, accommodating longer and higher resolution content.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#api-rate-limits)

API Rate Limits
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To maintain the quality of service and availability for all users, our API enforces rate limits based on the type of subscription plan.

| Plan | API Rate Limit |
| --- | --- |
| Free / Pro | 50 requests per day |
| Business / Enterprise | 60 requests per min |

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#add-to-live-api-rate-limit)

Add to Live API Rate Limit

The Add to Live API has a rate limit of 3 requests per 20 minutes.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#navigating-api-rate-limits)

Navigating API Rate Limits

*   **Free and Pro Plans:** These plans are ideal for light to moderate usage, with a cap of 50 API requests per day. This rate is suitable for testing and small-scale applications.
*   **Business and Enterprise Plans:** Designed for more demanding use cases, these plans allow up to 60 requests per minute, providing ample capacity for larger applications and higher volume demands.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

------------\
\
Use the API to upload audio to Fireflies.ai](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/upload-audio)

# Introspection - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Navigation

Fundamentals

Introspection

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#overview)
    
*   [Requirements](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#requirements)
    
*   [Introspection using Apollo Sandbox](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#introspection-using-apollo-sandbox)
    
*   [Introspection using Postman](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#introspection-using-postman)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Introspection is a feature that allows querying a GraphQL server to discover its schema. This capability is crucial for developers to understand available queries, mutations, and the structure of the data they can work with, facilitating seamless API interaction and exploration.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#requirements)

Requirements

You will need a Fireflies.ai API key to use introspection. For more details, please visit [Authorization](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#acquiring-a-token)

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#introspection-using-apollo-sandbox)

Introspection using Apollo Sandbox

For introspection using our builtin Apollo Sandbox, visit [api.fireflies.ai/graphql](https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql)
 and enter your `api_key` in the Headers section as a Bearer token

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#introspection-using-postman)

Introspection using Postman

Create a new Graphql Request in Postman with the url [api.fireflies.ai/graphql](https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql)
 and enter your `api_key` in the Headers section as a Bearer token

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/introspection#additional-resources)

# Super Admin - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Fundamentals

Super Admin

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#overview)
    
*   [Super Admin Webhooks](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#super-admin-webhooks)
    
*   [Setting up Super Admin Webhooks](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#setting-up-super-admin-webhooks)
    
*   [Privacy Settings Bypass](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#privacy-settings-bypass)
    
*   [Requirements](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#requirements)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Super Admin API offers advanced features such as team-wide webhooks and privacy setting bypass, providing enhanced control and flexibility for managing your data. This is only available on the enterprise tier for company admins - [learn more](https://guide.fireflies.ai/hc/en-us/articles/30453010621585-Learn-about-the-Super-Admin-role)
.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#super-admin-webhooks)

Super Admin Webhooks
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Super Admin webhook notifies you of all team meetings owned by your team, allowing you to automate workflows, integrate with other tools, and maintain an overview of your team’s meetings with a single webhook.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#setting-up-super-admin-webhooks)

Setting up Super Admin Webhooks

Follow the steps below to set up the Super Admin webhook:

1

Visit the [Fireflies.ai dashboard settings](https://app.fireflies.ai/settings)

2

Navigate to the Developer settings tab

3

Enter a valid https URL in the webhooks field and save

It is highly suggested to use [webhook auth](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks)
 to secure your servers.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#privacy-settings-bypass)

Privacy Settings Bypass

The Super Admin functionality allows you to bypass your team’s privacy settings, allowing you to query all data in your team’s account.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#requirements)

Requirements

Super Admin API is only available to teams on the Enterprise plan. [Learn more here](https://guide.fireflies.ai/hc/en-us/articles/30453010621585-Learn-about-the-Super-Admin-role)
 and reach out to us with questions

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin#additional-resources)

Additional Resources

--------\
\
Create notifications using webhooks](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks)

-------------\
\
Authenticating your requests with the Fireflies API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)

# Authorization - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Fundamentals

Authorization

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#overview)
    
*   [Token-Based Authentication](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#token-based-authentication)
    
*   [Acquiring a Token](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#acquiring-a-token)
    
*   [Making an Authenticated Request](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#making-an-authenticated-request)
    
*   [Example of an Authenticated Request Header](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#example-of-an-authenticated-request-header)
    
*   [Example request with Authorization header](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#example-request-with-authorization-header)
    
*   [Best Practices for Token Security](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#best-practices-for-token-security)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#troubleshooting)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#faq)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Fireflies API implements token-based authentication, which ensures that only authorized users can access certain data and functionalities.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#token-based-authentication)

Token-Based Authentication

We use a standard bearer token authentication mechanism. This means that to make authorized requests to the API, you must include an `Authorization` header with a valid token.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#acquiring-a-token)

Acquiring a Token

Follow these steps to obtain your API key for the Fireflies API:

1.  Log in to your account at [fireflies.ai](https://app.fireflies.ai/)
    
2.  Navigate to the [Integrations](https://app.fireflies.ai/integrations)
     section
3.  Click on [Fireflies API](https://app.fireflies.ai/integrations/custom/fireflies)
    
4.  Copy and store your API key securely

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#making-an-authenticated-request)

Making an Authenticated Request

To make an authenticated request, add the `Authorization` header followed by the word `Bearer` and your API key.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#example-of-an-authenticated-request-header)

Example of an Authenticated Request Header

Copy

Ask AI

    Authorization: Bearer your_api_key
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#example-request-with-authorization-header)

Example request with Authorization header

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

     curl \
       -X POST \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
       --data '{ "query": "{ user { name integrations } }" }' \
       https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Ensure to replace `your_api_key` with your actual API key.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#best-practices-for-token-security)

Best Practices for Token Security
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Keep it Secret:** Treat your API key like a password. Never expose it in client-side code or share it publicly.
*   **Store Securely:** Store the API key securely in your application, ideally in environment variables or secure storage solutions.

Improper handling of API keys can lead to security vulnerabilities. Always ensure API keys are used and stored securely.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Invalid key:** If you receive an error regarding an invalid API key, verify that the API key hasn’t expired and that it’s correctly included in the request header.
*   **Missing key:** Ensure that the `Authorization` header is present in your requests requiring authentication.

If you encounter issues with authentication or have questions about API key management, please contact our support team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#faq)

FAQ
--------------------------------------------------------------------

Why am I getting an 'auth\_failed' error?

This error can signal an issue in your Authorization header. Please ensure that you are including the `Authorization` header with the word `Bearer` and your API key.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

----------\
\
Make your first request in under 5 minutes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart)
[Errors\
------\
\
Error standards for the Fireflies API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors)

# Errors - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Fundamentals

Errors

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#overview)
    
*   [Error schema](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#error-schema)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Understanding how errors are structured and returned by the Fireflies API is key to effectively handling and troubleshooting issues. This page outlines the common error format and details specific error types.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#error-schema)

Error schema
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our GraphQL API follows a standard format for returning errors. Errors are encapsulated within an `errors` array in the response body. Please visit [Error codes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
 to view explanations for error code types

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#param-message)

message

String

required

Description of the error

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#param-code)

code

String

required

Error code.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#param-friendly)

friendly

Boolean

required

`friendly === true` are safe to show to the frontend client. Unfriendly errors may have technical details that may not be useful to the UI layer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#param-extensions)

extensions

Object

Contains useful metadata related to the error.Where relevant, includes field `helpUrls` pointing to relevant API documentation sections that explain the error and provide guidance on how to resolve it

Example

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {},
      "errors": [\
        {\
          "message": "Error description",\
    	    "friendly": true,\
          "code": "error_code",\
          "extensions": {\
            "helpUrls": [\
             "https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes#error_code"\
            ],\
            "code": "error_code",\
            "status": http_status_code,\
    		    ... otherFields\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/errors#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----------\
\
Detailed error code reference](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
[Authorization\
-------------\
\
Authenticating your requests with the Fireflies API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)

# Realtime API Overview - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Realtime API

Overview

On this page

*   [How It Works](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#how-it-works)
    
*   [Flow](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#flow)
    
*   [Features](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#features)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#additional-resources)
    

The Fireflies.ai Realtime API allows your application to receive **live transcription events** over WebSockets. This enables building interactive features such as live captioning, transcription overlays, and real-time analysis as users speak.

The Realtime API is currently in **beta**. Features and endpoints may change. We welcome your feedback as we continue to improve this API.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#how-it-works)

How It Works
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Realtime API uses WebSocket connections to deliver transcription data as it’s generated.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#flow)

Flow
-----------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Authenticate**: Connect using a valid API token and transcript ID.
2.  **Listen**: Once connected, you’ll start receiving transcription events in real time.
3.  **React**: Update your UI or process transcription events as they arrive.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#features)

Features
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Low Latency**: Data is streamed as soon as it’s transcribed.
*   **Event-Based**: Receive structured events for easy handling.
*   **Token-Based Authentication**: Secure connections with scoped access.
*   **Incremental Transcription**: Receive transcript segments progressively.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Getting Started\
---------------\
\
Getting Started with Realtime API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started)
[Event Schema\
------------\
\
Schema for Realtime Events](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema)

# Realtime API Events Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Realtime API

Event Schema

On this page

*   [Event Reference](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#event-reference)
    
*   [Event List](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#event-list)
    
*   [RealtimeTranscriptionEvent](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#realtimetranscriptionevent)
    
*   [Example Payload](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#example-payload)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#event-reference)

Event Reference
===========================================================================================

This page documents the events you may receive from the Fireflies.ai Realtime API WebSocket.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#event-list)

Event List
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Event Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `auth.success` | Emitted when authentication succeeds. |
| `auth.failed` | Emitted when authentication fails. The socket will disconnect after this event. |
| `connection.established` | Emitted when the connection is successfully established. |
| `connection.error` | Emitted when there is a connection or authorization error. |
| `transcription.broadcast` | Emitted for every new transcription segment or update. |

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#realtimetranscriptionevent)

RealtimeTranscriptionEvent
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-transcript-id)

transcript\_id

String

The unique identifier for the transcript / meeting

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-chunk-id)

chunk\_id

String

The unique identifier for the transcription segment (chunk). You may use this field to deduplicate transcription events. If the transcription is being updated, it will contain the same chunk\_id as the previous event. A new transcription will have a different chunk\_id

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-text)

text

String

The transcribed text for this segment.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-speaker-name)

speaker\_name

String

The name of the speaker for this segment.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-start-time)

start\_time

Float

The start time (in seconds)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#param-end-time)

end\_time

Float

The end time (in seconds)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#example-payload)

Example Payload
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "transcript_id": "abc123",
      "chunk_id": "chunk_001",
      "text": "Hello world",
      "speaker_name": "Alice",
      "start_time": 0.0,
      "end_time": 1.25
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/event-schema#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Getting Started\
---------------\
\
Getting started with Realtime API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started)
[Sentence\
--------\
\
Schema for Sentence](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/sentence)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

⌘K

Navigation

Getting Started

Quickstart

On this page

*   [Step 1: Setting Up](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-1%3A-setting-up)
    
*   [Obtaining Authentication Credentials](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#obtaining-authentication-credentials)
    
*   [Step 2: Making Your First Request](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-2%3A-making-your-first-request)
    
*   [Step 3: Analyzing the Response](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-3%3A-analyzing-the-response)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#additional-resources)
    

This guide provides step-by-step instructions to make your first query with our GraphQL API and demonstrates basic functionality.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-1%3A-setting-up)

Step 1: Setting Up
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before diving into querying the API, it’s essential to set up your environment correctly. This includes obtaining authentication credentials and configuring your development environment.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#obtaining-authentication-credentials)

Obtaining Authentication Credentials

To access our API, you will need an API key. Follow these steps to obtain your key:

1.  Log in to your account at [app.fireflies.ai](https://app.fireflies.ai/)
    
2.  Navigate to the [Integrations](https://app.fireflies.ai/integrations)
     section
3.  Click on [Fireflies API](https://app.fireflies.ai/integrations/custom/fireflies)
    
4.  Copy and store your API key securely

It’s crucial to handle your API key with the utmost care to ensure the security of your data. For more information on Authorization and best practices, visit [Authorization](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-2%3A-making-your-first-request)

Step 2: Making Your First Request
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Execute a simple query to retrieve a list of users. Replace `your_api_key` with your API key in the following requests

curl

python

javascript

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl \
       -X POST \
       -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
       -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
       --data '{ "query": "{ users { name user_id } }" }' \
       https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

  

When building GraphQL queries for this API, focus on precision and efficiency. Start with simple queries and gradually increase complexity. Ensure you only request the data you need to avoid over-fetching.

*   **Review the Schema Documentation**: For guidance, refer to the [Schema](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema)
     section and use tools like GraphQL Playground for testing. Efficient queries lead to better performance and a smoother API experience.

More details on building your GraphQL query are available [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#step-3%3A-analyzing-the-response)

Step 3: Analyzing the Response
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You will receive a JSON response with the requested data. Example response:

curl

Copy

Ask AI

    {
    	"data":
    	{
    		"users": [\
    			{\
    				"name":"Justin Fly",\
    				"user_id":"example-id"\
    			}\
    		]
    	}
    }
    

Continue to the next sections for more detailed examples and advanced usage instructions.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/getting-started/quickstart#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----\

# Realtime API Guide - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Realtime API

Getting Started

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#overview)
    
*   [Endpoint](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#endpoint)
    
*   [Requirements](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#requirements)
    
*   [Connecting via Socket.IO](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#connecting-via-socket-io)
    
*   [Auth Parameters](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#auth-parameters)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide shows you how to connect to the Fireflies.ai Realtime API and start receiving transcription events in real time.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#endpoint)

Endpoint
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    wss://api.fireflies.ai
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#requirements)

Requirements
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You’ll need the following:

*   A valid API token
*   A `transcriptId` (or meeting ID)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#connecting-via-socket-io)

Connecting via Socket.IO
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the Socket.IO client to connect and listen for events.

Copy

Ask AI

    import { io } from 'socket.io-client';
    
    const socket = io('wss://api.fireflies.ai', {
      path: '/ws/realtime',
      auth: {
        token: 'Bearer <YOUR_API_TOKEN>',
        transcriptId: '<TRANSCRIPT_ID>'
      }
    });
    
    socket.on('auth.success', data => {
      console.log('Authenticated:', data);
    });
    
    socket.on('auth.failed', err => {
      console.error('Authentication failed:', err);
    });
    
    socket.on('connection.error', err => {
      console.error('Connection error:', err);
    });
    
    socket.on('connection.established', () => {
      console.log('Connection established');
    });
    
    socket.on('transcription.broadcast', event => {
      console.log('Transcript event:', event);
    });
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#auth-parameters)

Auth Parameters
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token` | string | Your API access token |
| `transcriptId` | string | ID of the meeting or transcript |

If authentication fails, the server emits an `auth.failed` event and disconnects the socket. See [Authorization](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/getting-started#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Overview\
--------\
\
Overview of Realtime API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/realtime-api/overview)
[Authorization\
-------------\
\
Authenticating your requests with the Fireflies API](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/authorization)

Schema

MeetingInfo

On this page

*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info#param-fred-joined)

fred\_joined

Boolean

Boolean value that returns `true` if the bot joined the call, `false` otherwise.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info#param-silent-meeting)

silent\_meeting

Boolean

Boolean value that returns `true` if the meeting does not contain any spoken words. Otherwise false.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info#param-summary-status)

summary\_status

SummaryStatus

String value representing the summary status. Possible values are `processing`, `processed`, `failed`, `skipped`.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info#additional-resources)

Int

count\_diff\_pct

Int

# Advanced API Examples - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

Navigation

Examples

Advanced

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#overview)
    
*   [Find questions from external participants](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#find-questions-from-external-participants)
    
*   [Fetch meetings from multiple users](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#fetch-meetings-from-multiple-users)
    
*   [Verify webhook requests](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#verify-webhook-requests)
    
*   [Fireflies.ai Replit](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#fireflies-ai-replit)
    
*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore advanced usage examples that build on top of the Fireflies.ai API. This page is regularly updated

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#find-questions-from-external-participants)

[Find questions from external participants](https://replit.com/@firefliesai/Firefliesai-Find-questions-from-external-participants?v=1)

This replit allows you to query questions asked by participants who do not belong to your organization. It can be useful in deriving insights and analysis for client calls, interviews, etc.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#fetch-meetings-from-multiple-users)

[Fetch meetings from multiple users](https://replit.com/@firefliesai/Firefliesai-Fetch-meetings-for-multiple-users?v=1)

This replit allows you to fetch meetings from multiple users by providing it a list of API keys. Please read our privacy policy and terms of usage for more details

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#verify-webhook-requests)

[Verify webhook requests](https://replit.com/@firefliesai/Firefliesai-Verifying-webhook-requests?v=1)

This replit allows you to verify webhook requests by checking the signature and the payload.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#fireflies-ai-replit)

Fireflies.ai Replit
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the complete list of usage examples at [replit.com/@firefliesai](https://replit.com/@firefliesai)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/advanced#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------\
\
Basic usage examples](https://docs.fireflies.ai/examples/basic)
[Webhooks\
--------\
\
Create notifications using webhooks](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks)

# Summary Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Schema

Summary

On this page

*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#additional-resources)
    

Meeting AI summary prompts are defined by [AI apps](https://app.fireflies.ai/apps)
 and can be customized to your needs.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-action-items)

action\_items

String

A list of action items generated by the AI based on the meeting transcript

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-keywords)

keywords

String

A list of keywords generated by the AI based on the meeting transcript

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-outline)

outline

String

An outline of the meeting with timestamps generated by the AI based on the meeting transcript

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-overview)

overview

String

A summary of the meeting generated by the AI

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-shorthand-bullet)

shorthand\_bullet

String

A list of shorthand bullets generated by the AI

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-notes)

notes

String

Detailed meeting notes generated by the AI

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-gist)

gist

String

A summary of the meeting in 1 sentence

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-bullet-gist)

bullet\_gist

String

Summary of the meeting in a few bullet points with descriptive emojis

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-short-summary)

short\_summary

String

Summary of the meeting in a single paragraph

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-short-overview)

short\_overview

String

Brief overview of the meeting

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-meeting-type)

meeting\_type

String

Meeting classification

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-topics-discussed)

topics\_discussed

\[String\]

List of topics discussed during the meeting.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-transcript-chapters)

transcript\_chapters

\[String\]

Chapters of the short transcript. The short transcript is an LLM-condensed transcript that may be helpful for downstream applications

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#param-extended-sections)

extended\_sections

\[SummarySection\]

Optional sections of the summary included by customizing the summary from the dashboard

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Summary Section\
---------------\
\
Schema for Summary Section](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary-section)
[Transcript\
----------\
\
Schema for Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript)

# Deprecated - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Additional Info

Deprecated

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#overview)
    
*   [Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#transcript)
    
*   [Transcripts](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#transcripts)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page lists all the fields that have been deprecated. Deprecated fields are fields that are no longer recommended for use and may be removed in future versions.

Please note that using deprecated fields can lead to compatibility issues in future releases.

The following fields have been deprecated:

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#transcript)

[Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript)

`host_email`: Use `organizer_email` instead.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated#transcripts)

[Transcripts](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts)

`date`: Use `fromDate` and `toDate` to query a time range. `title`: Use `keyword` and `scope` instead of `title` `organizer_email`: Use the `organizers` array field to filter by one or more organizer email addresses. `participant_email`: Use the `participants` array field to filter by one or more participant email addresses.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Webhooks enable your application to set up event based notifications. In this section, you’ll learn how to configure webhooks to receive updates from Fireflies.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#events-supported)

Events supported
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The webhooks support the following events:

*   Transcription complete: Triggers when a meeting has been processed and the transcript is ready for viewing

Fireflies sends webhook notifications as POST requests to your specified endpoint. Each request contains a JSON payload with information about the event that occurred.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#saving-a-webhook)

Saving a webhook
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Follow the instructions below to save a webhook URL that sends notifications for all subscribed events. This webhook will only be fired for meetings that you own.

1

Visit the [Fireflies.ai dashboard settings](https://app.fireflies.ai/settings)

2

Navigate to the Developer settings tab

3

Enter a valid https URL in the webhooks field and save

You may test your webhook using the upload audio API or by uploading through the dashboard at [app.fireflies.ai/upload](https://app.fireflies.ai/upload)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#upload-audio-webhook)

Upload audio webhook
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also include a webhook URL as part of an upload audio request. This is different from the saved webhook as it will only send notifications for that singular audio upload request.

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
      -d '{
        "query": "mutation($input: AudioUploadInput) { uploadAudio(input: $input) { success title message } }",
        "variables": {
          "input": {
            "url": "https://url_to_the_audio_file",
            "title": "title of the file",
            "webhook": "https://url_for_the_webhook"
          }
        }
      }' \
      https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#webhook-authentication)

Webhook Authentication
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Webhook authentication ensures that incoming webhook requests are securely verified before processing. This allows consumers to trust that webhook events originate from a secure and verified source.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#how-it-works)

How It Works

Each webhook request sent from the server includes an `x-hub-signature` header containing a SHA-256 HMAC signature of the request payload. This signature is generated using a secret key known only to the server and your application. When the consumer receives a webhook, they can use the signature provided in the `x-hub-signature` header to verify that the request has not been tampered with. This is done by computing their own HMAC signature using the shared secret key and comparing it to the signature included in the header.

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#saving-a-secret)

Saving a secret

1.  Go to the settings page at [app.fireflies.ai/settings](https://app.fireflies.ai/settings)
    
2.  Navigate to the **Developer Settings** tab
3.  You can either:
    *   Enter a custom secret key of 16-32 characters in the input field
    *   Click on the refresh button to generate a random secret key
4.  Click Save to ensure the secret gets updated
5.  Make sure to store this secret key securely, as it will be used to authenticate incoming webhook requests

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#verifying-the-signature)

Verifying the Signature

1.  **Receive the Webhook**:
    *   Each request will include the payload and an `x-hub-signature` header
2.  **Verify the Signature**:
    *   Compute the HMAC SHA-256 signature using the payload and the shared secret key
    *   Compare the computed signature to the `x-hub-signature` header value
    *   If they match, the request is verified as authentic. If they do not match, treat the request with caution or reject it

By verifying webhook signatures, consumers can ensure that webhook events received are secure and have not been altered during transmission

### 

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#see-it-in-action)

See it in action

To see webhook authentication in action, you can view an example at [Fireflies.ai Verifying Webhook Requests](https://replit.com/@firefliesai/Firefliesai-Verifying-webhook-requests#index.js)
. This example demonstrates how to receive a webhook, compute the HMAC SHA-256 signature, and verify it against the `x-hub-signature` header to ensure the request’s authenticity.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#webhook-schema)

Webhook Schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#param-meeting-id)

meetingId

String

required

Identifier for the meeting / transcript that the webhook has triggered for. MeetingId and TranscriptId are used interchangeably for the Fireflies.ai Platform.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#param-event-type)

eventType

String

Name of the event type that has been fired against the webhook

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#param-client-reference-id)

clientReferenceId

ID

Custom identifier set by the user during upload. You may use this to identify your uploads in your events.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#example-payload)

Example Payload
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "meetingId": "ASxwZxCstx",
      "eventType": "Transcription completed",
      "clientReferenceId": "be582c46-4ac9-4565-9ba6-6ab4264496a8"
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#faq)

FAQ
--------------------------------------------------------------

Why am I not receiving webhook requests

There may be multiple reasons why you are not receiving webhook requests. Please go through the following checklist:

*   Webhooks are only fired for meeting owners, referred to in the API as the `organizer_email.` Ensure that you have correctly setup the webhooks for the meeting owner.
*   Ensure that your webhook is setup as a POST request
*   If you have setup secret verification, ensure that you are correctly verifying the request by checking the example implementation [here](https://replit.com/@firefliesai/Firefliesai-Verifying-webhook-requests?v=1)
    .

Team-wide webhooks are only supported for the Enterprise tier with the Super Admin role. This allows you to setup one webhook for all meetings owned by your team. Details [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/super-admin)
.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks#additional-resources)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/bite#param-privacies)

privacies

\[BitePrivacy\]

Array specifying the visibility of the Bite. Possible values are `public`, `team`, and `participants`. For example, `["team", "participants"]` indicates visibility to both team members and participants, while `["public"]` allows anyone to access the bite through its link

)

String

Int

String

String

Details about the user’s most recent meeting.

Int

Total number of minutes consumed by the user in meetings.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/user#param-is-admin)

is\_admin

Boolean

Indicates whether the user has administrative privileges. True if the user is an admin, false otherwise.

A list of integrations enabled for the user’s account.

# Transcript Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Schema

Transcript

On this page

*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-id)

id

ID

Unique identifier of the Transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-title)

title

String

Title of the Transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-host-email)

host\_email

String

[DEPRECATED](https://docs.fireflies.ai/additional-info/deprecated)
  
Email address of the meeting host.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-organizer-email)

organizer\_email

String

Email address of the meeting organizer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-user)

user

User

The [User](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/user)
 who Fred recorded the meeting on behalf of

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-speakers)

speakers

\[Speaker\]

The speakers array contains the id and name of the speaker as it appears within the transcript

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-transcript-url)

transcript\_url

String

The url to view the transcript in the dashboard

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-participants)

participants

\[String\]

An array of email addresses of meeting participants guests, including participants that do not have Fireflies account.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-meeting-attendees)

meeting\_attendees

\[MeetingAttendee\]

List of [MeetingAttendee](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendee)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-meeting-attendance)

meeting\_attendance

\[MeetingAttendance\]

List of [MeetingAttendance](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance)
 records showing when participants joined and left the meeting

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-fireflies-users)

fireflies\_users

\[String\]

An array of email addresses of only Fireflies users participants that have fireflies account that participated in the meeting

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-duration)

duration

Number

Duration of the audio in minutes

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-date-string)

dateString

DateTime

String representation of DateTime. Example: `2024-04-22T20:14:04.454Z`

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-date)

date

Float

Date the transcript was created represented in milliseconds from [EPOCH](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Epoch_(computing))
.The timezone for this field is UTC +00:00

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-audio-url)

audio\_url

String

Secure, newly generated hashed url that allows you download meeting audio. This url expires after every 24 hours. You’d have to make another request to generate a new audio\_url.You need to be subscribed to subscribed to a pro or higher plan to query audio\_url. View plans [here](https://fireflies.ai/pricing)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-video-url)

video\_url

String

Secure, newly generated hashed url that allows you download meeting video. This url expires after every 24 hours. You’d have to make another request to generate a new video\_url. You will need to enable `RECORD MEETING VIDEO` setting on your Fireflies [dashboard](https://app.fireflies.ai/settings)
 for this to work.You need to be subscribed to a business or higher plan to query video\_url. View plans [here](https://fireflies.ai/pricing)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-sentence)

sentence

\[Sentence\]

An array of [Sentence](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/sentence)
(s), containing transcript details like `raw_text`, `speaker_name`, etc.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-calendar-id)

calendar\_id

String

Calendar provider event ID. This field represents calId for google calendar and iCalUID for outlook calendar.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-summary)

summary

Summary

AI generated [Summary](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary)
 of the meeting.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-meeting-info)

meeting\_info

MeetingInfo

[MeetingInfo](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-info)
 metadata fields.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-cal-id)

cal\_id

String

Calendar provider event ID with a timestamp that helps uniquely identify recurring events

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-calendar-type)

calendar\_type

String

Calendar provider name

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-apps)

apps

Apps

Preview of [Apps](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/apps)
 generated from the transcript. Max limit of 5 most recent AI App Outputs per meeting. Use the [Apps Query](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps)
 to fetch the entire list of AI App Outputs

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-meeting-link)

meeting\_link

String

The web conferencing url of the meeting. This field is only populated if the meeting was hosted on a supported platform such as Google Meet, Zoom, etc.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-analytics)

analytics

MeetingAnalytics

[MeetingAnalytics](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-analytics)
 contains analytics data about the meeting, including:

*   `sentiments`: Sentiment analysis showing percentages of positive, neutral, and negative sentiments
*   `categories`: Counts of different types of content (questions, date/times, metrics, tasks)
*   `speakers`: Detailed analytics for each speaker including duration, word count, filler words, etc.

You need to be subscribed to subscribed to a pro or higher plan to query meeting analytics. View plans [here](https://fireflies.ai/pricing)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#param-channels)

channels

\[Channel\]

An array of [Channel](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/channel)
 the meeting belongs to

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Summary\
-------\
\
Schema for Summary](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/summary)
[Sentence\
--------\
\
Schema for Sentence](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/sentence)
