[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/upload-audio#faq)

FAQ
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Can I upload a file directly from my machine?

Audio upload only works with publicly accessible URLs. We cannot accept files hosted on your local machine or a private server.

I don't want to expose my audio files to the public internet. How can I upload them to Fireflies.ai safely?

You may use signed urls with short expiry times to upload audio files to Fireflies.ai. Fireflies will download the file from the url and process it.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/upload-audio#error-codes)

Error Codes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `uploadAudio` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

account\_cancelled

The user account has been cancelled. Please contact support if you encounter this error.

paid\_required (pro\_or\_higher)

You may receieve this error when uploading audio files or querying `audio_url` field.

Free plan users cannot upload audio files. Please upgrade to a paid plan to upload audio files.

paid\_required (business\_or\_higher)

You may receieve this error when querying `video_url` field.

Free/pro plan users cannot query `video_url` field. Please upgrade to a Business or Enterprise plan to query `video_url` field.

payload\_too\_small

The audio file is too short to be processed. Please ensure the audio file is at least 50kb in size.

invalid\_language\_code

The language code you provided is invalid. Please refer to the [Language Codes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/language-codes)
 page for a list of valid language codes.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/upload-audio#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Webhooks\
--------\
\
Create notifications using webhooks](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/webhooks)

-----------\

Use the API to add the Fireflies.ai bot to an ongoing meeting](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live)

# MeetingAttendance Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

MeetingAttendance

On this page

*   [Additional Resources](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#additional-resources)
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#param-name)

name

String

Name of the meeting participant as it appears in the meeting events.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#param-join-time)

join\_time

String

ISO 8601 timestamp when the participant first joined the meeting. If the participant joined at meeting start (timestamp: 0), this will be the meeting’s start time.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#param-leave-time)

leave\_time

String

ISO 8601 timestamp when the participant last left the meeting. This field is nullable if the participant never left or the leave event was not captured.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendance#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MeetingAttendee\
---------------\
\
Schema for MeetingAttendee](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/meeting-attendee)
[Transcript\
----------\
\
Schema for Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript)

# Transcript query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Query

Transcript

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query Transcript($transcriptId: String!) { transcript(id: $transcriptId) { title id } }", "variables": { "transcriptId": "your_transcript_id" } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "transcript": {
          "title": "Weekly sync",
          "id": "transcript-id",
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The transcript query is designed to fetch details associated with a specific transcript ID.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#arguments)

Arguments
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#param-id)

id

String

required

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#schema)

Schema
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#usage-example)

Usage Example
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query Transcript($transcriptId: String!) {
      transcript(id: $transcriptId) {
        id
        dateString
        privacy
        analytics {
          sentiments {
            negative_pct
            neutral_pct
            positive_pct
          }
          categories {
            questions
            date_times
            metrics
            tasks
          }
          speakers {
            speaker_id
            name
            duration
            word_count
            longest_monologue
            monologues_count
            filler_words
            questions
            duration_pct
            words_per_minute
          }
        }
        speakers {
          id
          name
        }
        sentences {
          index
          speaker_name
          speaker_id
          text
          raw_text
          start_time
          end_time
          ai_filters {
            task
            pricing
            metric
            question
            date_and_time
            text_cleanup
            sentiment
          }
        }
        title
        host_email
        organizer_email
        calendar_id
        user {
          user_id
          email
          name
          num_transcripts
          recent_meeting
          minutes_consumed
          is_admin
          integrations
        }
        fireflies_users
        participants
        date
        transcript_url
        audio_url
        video_url
        duration
        meeting_attendees {
          displayName
          email
          phoneNumber
          name
          location
        }
        meeting_attendance {
          name
          join_time
          leave_time
        }
        summary {
          keywords
          action_items
          outline
          shorthand_bullet
          overview
          bullet_gist
          gist
          short_summary
          short_overview
          meeting_type
          topics_discussed
          transcript_chapters
        }
        cal_id
        calendar_type
        meeting_info {
          fred_joined
          silent_meeting
          summary_status
        }
        apps_preview {
          outputs {
            transcript_id
            user_id
            app_id
            created_at
            title
            prompt
            response
          }
        }
        meeting_link
        channels {
          id
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query Transcript($transcriptId: String!) { transcript(id: $transcriptId) { title id } }", "variables": { "transcriptId": "your_transcript_id" } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "transcript": {
          "title": "Weekly sync",
          "id": "transcript-id",
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#error-codes)

Error Codes
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `transcript` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

object\_not\_found (transcript)

The transcript ID you are trying to query does not exist or you do not have access to it.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript#additional-resources)

# AI Apps query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Query

AI Apps

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query GetAIAppsOutputs($transcriptId: String) { apps(transcript_id: $transcriptId) { outputs { transcript_id user_id app_id created_at title prompt response } } }", "variables": { "transcriptId": "your_transcript_id" } }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "apps": [\
    		{\
    			"transcript_id": "transcript-id",\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"app_id": "app-id",\
    			"title": "Weekly sync"\
    		}\
    	]
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

The apps query fetches the results of the AI App for all the meetings it ran successfully.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#arguments)

Arguments
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#param-app-id)

app\_id

String

The `app_id` parameter retrieves all outputs against a specific AI App.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#param-transcript-id)

transcript\_id

String

The `transcript_id` parameter retrieves all outputs against a specific meeting/transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#param-skip)

skip

Int

Number of records to skip over. Helps paginate results when used in combination with the `limit` param.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#param-limit)

limit

Int

Maximum number of `apps` outputs to fetch in a single query. The default query fetches 10 records, which is the maximum for a single request.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#schema)

Schema
----------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [AI Apps](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/apps)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#usage-example)

Usage Example
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query GetAIAppsOutputs($appId: String, $transcriptId: String, $skip: Float, $limit: Float) {
      apps(app_id: $appId, transcript_id: $transcriptId, skip: $skip, limit: $limit) {
        outputs {
          transcript_id
          user_id
          app_id
          created_at
          title
          prompt
          response
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query GetAIAppsOutputs($transcriptId: String) { apps(transcript_id: $transcriptId) { outputs { transcript_id user_id app_id created_at title prompt response } } }", "variables": { "transcriptId": "your_transcript_id" } }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "apps": [\
    		{\
    			"transcript_id": "transcript-id",\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"app_id": "app-id",\
    			"title": "Weekly sync"\
    		}\
    	]
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/apps#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

----------\
\
Querying transcript details](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcript)

\

# User Groups query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Query

User Groups

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "{ user_groups { name handle members { first_name last_name email } } }" }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "user_groups": [\
          {\
            "id": "group_123",\
            "name": "Engineering Team",\
            "handle": "engineering",\
            "members": [\
              {\
                "user_id": "user_456",\
                "first_name": "John",\
                "last_name": "Doe",\
                "email": "john.doe@example.com"\
              },\
              {\

                "first_name": "Jane",\
                "last_name": "Smith",\
                "email": "jane.smith@example.com"\

            ]\

          {\
            "id": "group_124",\
            "name": "Sales Team",\
            "handle": "sales",\
            "members": [\
              {\
                "user_id": "user_101",\
                "first_name": "Bob",\
                "last_name": "Johnson",\
                "email": "bob.johnson@example.com"\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The user\_groups query is designed to fetch a list of all user groups within the team. This query allows you to retrieve information about user groups including their members.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#arguments)

Arguments
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#param-mine)

mine

Boolean

`mine` is an optional boolean argument. If set to `true`, returns only user groups that the current user belongs to. If not provided or set to `false`, returns all user groups in the team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#schema)

Schema
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [UserGroup](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/user-groups)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#usage-example)

Usage Example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query UserGroups($mine: Boolean) {
      user_groups(mine: $mine) {
        id
        name
        handle
        members {
          user_id
          first_name
          last_name
          email
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "{ user_groups { name handle members { first_name last_name email } } }" }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "user_groups": [\
          {\
            "id": "group_123",\
            "name": "Engineering Team",\
            "handle": "engineering",\
            "members": [\
              {\
                "user_id": "user_456",\
                "first_name": "John",\
                "last_name": "Doe",\
                "email": "john.doe@example.com"\
              },\
              {\
                "user_id": "user_789",\
                "first_name": "Jane",\
                "last_name": "Smith",\
                "email": "jane.smith@example.com"\
              }\
            ]\
          },\
          {\
            "id": "group_124",\
            "name": "Sales Team",\
            "handle": "sales",\
            "members": [\
              {\
                "user_id": "user_101",\
                "first_name": "Bob",\
                "last_name": "Johnson",\
                "email": "bob.johnson@example.com"\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#error-codes)

Error Codes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `user_groups` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

not\_authorized

You do not have permission to access user groups for this team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user-groups#additional-resources)

# Add to Live - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Mutation

Add to Live

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
      -d '{
        "query": "mutation AddToLiveMeeting($meetingLink: String!) { addToLiveMeeting(meeting_link: $meetingLink) { success } }",
        "variables": {
          "meetingLink": "https://meet.google.com/code-here"
        }
      }' \
      https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "addToLiveMeeting": {
          "success": true,
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `addToLiveMeeting` mutation allows you to add the Fireflies.ai bot to an ongoing meeting. It is rate limited to 3 requests per 20 minutes.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#arguments)

Arguments
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-meeting-link)

meeting\_link

String!

required

A valid http URL for the meeting link, i.e. gooogle meet, zoom, etc

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-title)

title

String

Title or name of the meeting, this will be used to identify the transcribed file. If title is not provided, a default title will be set automaticallyMaximum length is 256 characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-meeting-password)

meeting\_password

String

Password for the meeting, if applicable.Maximum length is 32 characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-duration)

duration

Int

Meeting duration in minutes. Defaults to 60 minutes if param is not providedMinimum is 15 and maximum is 120.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-language)

language

String

Language of the meeting. Defaults to English if not provided. For a complete list of language codes, please view [Language Codes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/language-codes)
Maximum length is 5 characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#param-attendees)

attendees

\[Attendee\]

Array of [Attendees](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/attendee)
 for expected meeting participants.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#usage-example)

Usage Example
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To upload an audio file, provide the necessary input parameters to the mutation. Here’s an example of how this mutation could be used:

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation AddToLiveMeeting($meetingLink: String!) {
      addToLiveMeeting(meeting_link: $meetingLink) {
        success
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
      -d '{
        "query": "mutation AddToLiveMeeting($meetingLink: String!) { addToLiveMeeting(meeting_link: $meetingLink) { success } }",
        "variables": {
          "meetingLink": "https://meet.google.com/code-here"
        }
      }' \
      https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "addToLiveMeeting": {
          "success": true,
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#faq)

FAQ
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Why am I getting a 'too\_many\_requests' error?

The `addToLive` mutation has a limit of 3 requests per 20 minutes.

You may view API Rate limits [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/fundamentals/limits)
.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#error-codes)

Error Codes
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `addToLiveMeeting` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

too\_many\_requests

You have exceeded the rate limit for the `addToLiveMeeting` mutation. It is limited to 3 requests per 20 minutes. Please try again later.

invalid\_language\_code

The language code you provided is invalid. Please refer to the [Language Codes](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/language-codes)
 page for a list of valid language codes.

account\_cancelled

The user account has been cancelled. Please contact support if you encounter this error.

unsupported\_platform

The meeting platform URL provided is not supported. Please use a supported meeting platform such as Zoom, Google Meet, Microsoft Teams, etc.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/add-to-live#additional-resources)

# UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-privacy-input#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Input

UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-privacy-input#param-id)

id

String

required

The unique identifier of the meeting / transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-privacy-input#param-privacy)

privacy

String

required

The privacy level for the meeting. Must be one of the following values:

*   `link` - Anyone with the link can access the meeting
*   `owner` - Only the meeting owner can access
*   `participants` - Only meeting participants can access
*   `teammatesandparticipants` - Both teammates and participants can access
*   `teammates` - Only teammates can access

# Transcripts query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Query

Transcripts

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query Transcripts($userId: String) { transcripts(user_id: $userId) { title id } }" }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "transcripts": [\
    		{\
    			"title": "Weekly sync",\
    			"id": "transcript-id",\
    		},\
    		{\
    			"title": "ClientMeeting.mp3",\
    			"id": "transcript-id-2",\
    		}\
    	]
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The transcripts query is designed to fetch a list of transcripts against input arguments.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#arguments)

Arguments
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-title)

title

String

**This field is deprecated. Please use `keyword` instead.**Title of the transcriptThis argument is mutually exclusive with `keyword` fieldThe maximum allowable length for this field is `256` characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-keyword)

keyword

String

Allows searching for keywords in meeting title and/or words spoken during the meetingThis argument is mutually exclusive with `title` fieldThe maximum allowable length for this field is `255` characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-scope)

scope

TranscriptsQueryScope

Specify the scope for keyword search.If scope is provided, `keyword` becomes a required fieldDefaults to `TITLE` if no value is providedThe available options for this field are:

*   `title`: Search within the title.
*   `sentences`: Search within the [sentences](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/sentence)
    .
*   `all`: Search within title and sentences.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-from-date)

fromDate

DateTime

Return all transcripts created after `fromDate`. The `fromDate` parameter accepts a date-time string in the ISO 8601 format, specifically in the form `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm.sssZ`. For example, a valid timestamp would be `2024-07-08T22:13:46.660Z`.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-to-date)

toDate

DateTime

Return all transcripts created before `toDate`. The `toDate` parameter accepts a date-time string in the ISO 8601 format, specifically in the form `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm.sssZ`. For example, a valid timestamp would be `2024-07-08T22:13:46.660Z`.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-date)

date

Float

**This field is deprecated. Please use `fromDate` and `toDate` instead.**Return all transcripts created within the date specified. Query input value must be in milliseconds. For example, you can use the JavaScript `new Date().getTime()` to get the datetime in milliseconds which should look like this `1621292557453`. The timezone for this field is UTC +00:00For more details regarding time since [EPOCH](https://currentmillis.com/)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-limit)

limit

Int

Number of transcripts to return. Maxiumum 50 in one query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-skip)

skip

Int

Number of transcripts to skip.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-host-email)

host\_email

String

Filter all meetings accordingly to meetings that have this email as the host.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-organizer-email)

organizer\_email

String

**This field is deprecated. Please use `organizers` instead.** Filter meetings that have this email as the organizer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-participant-email)

participant\_email

String

**This field is deprecated. Please use `participants` instead.** Filter meetings that contain this email as an attendee.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-user-id)

user\_id

String

[User id](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/user)
. Filter all meetings that have this user ID as the organizer or participant.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-mine)

mine

Boolean

Filter all meetings that have the API key owner as the organizer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-organizers)

organizers

\[String\]

Filter meetings that have any of these emails as organizers. Accepts an array of email addresses.Cannot be combined with the deprecated `organizer_email` or `participant_email` fields.Each email must be valid and 256 characters or fewer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-participants)

participants

\[String\]

Filter meetings that contain any of these emails as attendees. Accepts an array of email addresses.Cannot be combined with the deprecated `organizer_email` or `participant_email` fields.Each email must be valid and 256 characters or fewer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#param-channel-id)

channel\_id

String

Filter meetings that belong to a specific channel. Accepts a single channel ID.The channel ID must be a valid string and 256 characters or fewer.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#schema)

Schema
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [Transcript](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/transcript)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#usage-example)

Usage Example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query Transcripts(
      $title: String
      $date: Float
      $limit: Int
      $skip: Int
      $hostEmail: String
      $participantEmail: String
      $organizers: [String]
      $participants: [String]
      $userId: String
      $channelId: String
    ) {
      transcripts(
        title: $title
        date: $date
        limit: $limit
        skip: $skip
        host_email: $hostEmail
        participant_email: $participantEmail
        organizers: $organizers
        participants: $participants
        user_id: $userId
        channel_id: $channelId
      ) {
        id
        analytics {
          sentiments {
            negative_pct
            neutral_pct
            positive_pct
          }
          categories {
            questions
            date_times
            metrics
            tasks
          }
          speakers {
            speaker_id
            name
            duration
            word_count
            longest_monologue
            monologues_count
            filler_words
            questions
            duration_pct
            words_per_minute
          }
        }
        sentences {
          index
          speaker_name
          speaker_id
          text
          raw_text
          start_time
          end_time
          ai_filters {
            task
            pricing
            metric
            question
            date_and_time
            text_cleanup
            sentiment
          }
        }
        title
        speakers {
          id
          name
        }
        host_email
        organizer_email
        meeting_info {
          fred_joined
          silent_meeting
          summary_status
        }
        calendar_id
        user {
          user_id
          email
          name
          num_transcripts
          recent_meeting
          minutes_consumed
          is_admin
          integrations
        }
        fireflies_users
        participants
        date
        transcript_url
        audio_url
        video_url
        duration
        meeting_attendees {
          displayName
          email
          phoneNumber
          name
          location
        }
        meeting_attendance {
          name
          join_time
          leave_time
        }
        summary {
          keywords
          action_items
          outline
          shorthand_bullet
          overview
          bullet_gist
          gist
          short_summary
          short_overview
          meeting_type
          topics_discussed
          transcript_chapters
        }
        cal_id
        calendar_type
        apps_preview {
          outputs {
            transcript_id
            user_id
            app_id
            created_at
            title
            prompt
            response
          }
        }
        meeting_link
        channels {
          id
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query Transcripts($userId: String) { transcripts(user_id: $userId) { title id } }" }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "transcripts": [\
    		{\
    			"title": "Weekly sync",\
    			"id": "transcript-id",\
    		},\
    		{\
    			"title": "ClientMeeting.mp3",\
    			"id": "transcript-id-2",\
    		}\
    	]
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts#error-codes)

Error Codes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `transcripts` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

object\_not\_found (user)

The user ID you are trying to query does not exist or you do not have access to it.

# Update Meeting Title - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Navigation

Mutation

Update Meeting Title

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($input: UpdateMeetingTitleInput!) { updateMeetingTitle(input: $input) { title } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"input": {
    				"id": "your_transcript_id",
    				"title": "New Title"
    			}
    		}
    	}'

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "updateMeetingTitle": {
          "title": "New Title"
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `updateMeetingTitle` mutation allows for updating the title of a meeting transcript. This operation requires admin privileges within the team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#arguments)

Arguments
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#param-input)

input

UpdateMeetingTitleInput

required

The new title to be assigned to the meeting / transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#usage-example)

Usage Example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To update a meeting title, provide the transcript ID and the new title as arguments to the mutation. Here’s an example of how this mutation could be used:

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation UpdateMeetingTitle($input: UpdateMeetingTitleInput!) {
      updateMeetingTitle(input: $input) {
        title
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($input: UpdateMeetingTitleInput!) { updateMeetingTitle(input: $input) { title } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"input": {
    				"id": "your_transcript_id",
    				"title": "New Title"
    			}
    		}
    	}'
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "updateMeetingTitle": {
          "title": "New Title"
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#faq)

FAQ
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Who has permission to update meeting titles?

Only users with admin privileges can update meeting titles. The meeting owner also needs to be in your team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#error-codes)

Error Codes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `updateMeetingTitle` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

require\_elevated\_privilege

The user does not have admin privileges to update meeting titles.

object\_not\_found (transcript)

The specified transcript could not be found or you do not have access to it

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title#additional-resources)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\

----------------------\
\
Update meeting privacy](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

Navigation

Query

Bite

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query Bite($biteId: ID!) { bite(id: $biteId) { user_id name status summary } }", "variables": { "biteId": "your_bite_id" } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

          "user_id": "user-id",

      }

# Delete Transcript - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Mutation

Delete Transcript

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
      -d '{"query": "mutation($transcriptId: String!) { deleteTranscript(id: $transcriptId) { title date duration organizer_email } }", "variables": {"transcriptId": "your_transcript_id"}}' \
      https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "deleteTranscript": {
          "duration": "1",
          "date": 1699570138000,
          "organizer_email": "justin@fly.ai",
          "title": "Video title"
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `deleteTranscript` mutation is designed to delete a specific transcript by its ID.

**Rate Limit:** This mutation is rate-limited to 10 requests per minute across all user tiers. If you exceed this limit, you will receive a `too_many_requests` error with a `retryAfter` timestamp indicating when you can make requests again.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#arguments)

Arguments
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#param-id)

id

String

required

Transcript ID

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#usage-example)

Usage Example
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To delete a transcript, provide the unique id of the transcript as an argument to the mutation. The returned subfields will be from the deleted transcript. Here’s an example of how this mutation could be used:

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation deleteTranscript($id: String!) {
      deleteTranscript(id: $id) {
        id
        title
        host_email
        organizer_email
        fireflies_users
        participants
        date
        transcript_url
        audio_url
        duration
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
      -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
      -d '{"query": "mutation($transcriptId: String!) { deleteTranscript(id: $transcriptId) { title date duration organizer_email } }", "variables": {"transcriptId": "your_transcript_id"}}' \
      https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "deleteTranscript": {
          "duration": "1",
          "date": 1699570138000,
          "organizer_email": "justin@fly.ai",
          "title": "Video title"
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#error-codes)

Error Codes
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `deleteTranscript` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

require\_elevated\_privilege

The user does not have admin privileges to delete the transcript.

too\_many\_requests

You have exceeded the rate limit of 10 requests per minute. Wait until the time specified in the `retryAfter` field before making additional requests.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/delete-transcript#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Transcripts\
-----------\
\
Querying list of transcripts](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/transcripts)
[Update Meeting Privacy\
----------------------\
\
Update meeting privacy](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy)

# Bites query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Query

Bites

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query Bites($mine: Boolean) { bites(mine: $mine) { user_id name end_time } }", "variables": { "mine": true } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "bites": [\
    		{\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"id": "bite-id",\
        	},\
    		{\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"id": "bite-id-2",\
        	}\
    	]	
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#overview)

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The bites query is designed to fetch a list of bites against input arguments.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#arguments)

Arguments
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#param-mine)

mine

Boolean

required

The `mine` parameter, when set to true, fetches results specific to the owner of the API key

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#param-transcript-id)

transcript\_id

ID

You can use `transcript_id` to query all bites against a specific transcript.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#param-my-team)

my\_team

Boolean

The `my_team` parameter, when set to true, fetches results for the owner of the API key

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#param-limit)

limit

Int

Maximum number of bites to fetch in a single query. Maximum of 50

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#param-skip)

skip

Int

Number of records to skip over. Helps paginate results when used in combination with the `limit` param.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#schema)

Schema
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [Bites](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/bite)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#usage-example)

Usage Example
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query Bites($mine: Boolean) {
      bites(mine: $mine) {
        transcript_id
        name
        id
        thumbnail
        preview
        status
        summary
        user_id
        start_time
        end_time
        summary_status
        media_type
        created_at
        created_from {
          description
          duration
          id
          name
          type
        }
        captions {
          end_time
          index
          speaker_id
          speaker_name
          start_time
          text
        }
        sources {
          src
          type
        }
        privacies
        user {
          first_name
          last_name
          picture
          name
          id
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query Bites($mine: Boolean) { bites(mine: $mine) { user_id name end_time } }", "variables": { "mine": true } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "bites": [\
    		{\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"id": "bite-id",\
        	},\
    		{\
    			"user_id": "user-id",\
    			"id": "bite-id-2",\
        	}\
    	]	
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#error-codes)

Error Codes
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `bites` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

args\_required

You must provide at least one of the following arguments: `mine`, `transcript_id`, `my_team` to the bites query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/bites#additional-resources)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The users query is designed to fetch a list of all users within the team. You can also view this list on your dashboard at [app.fireflies.ai/team](http://app.fireflies.ai/team)

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/users#schema)

    query Users {
      users {
        user_id
        email
        name
        num_transcripts
        recent_meeting
        minutes_consumed
        is_admin
        integrations
        user_groups {
          id
          name
          handle
          members {
            user_id
            first_name
            last_name
            email
          }
        }
      }
    }

# Set User Role - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Mutation

Set User Role

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($user_id: String!, $role: Role!) { setUserRole(user_id: $user_id, role:$role) { name is_admin } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"user_id": "your_user_id",
    			"role": "admin"
    		}
    	}'

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "setUserRole": {
          "name": "Justin Fly",
          "is_admin": "true",
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `setUserRole` mutation allows for the updating of a user’s role within a team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#arguments)

Arguments
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#param-user-id)

user\_id

String

required

The unique identifier of the user.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#param-role)

role

Role

required

The [Role](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/role)
 to be assigned to the user. Valid types for user are `admin` and `user`

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#usage-example)

Usage Example
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To set a user’s role, provide the user’s ID and the desired role as arguments to the mutation. Here’s an example of how this mutation could be used:

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation setUserRole($userId: String!, $role: Role!) {
      setUserRole(user_id: $userId, role: $role) {
        id
        name
        email
        role
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($user_id: String!, $role: Role!) { setUserRole(user_id: $user_id, role:$role) { name is_admin } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"user_id": "your_user_id",
    			"role": "admin"
    		}
    	}'
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "setUserRole": {
          "name": "Justin Fly",
          "is_admin": "true",
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#error-codes)

Error Codes
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `setUserRole` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

object\_not\_found (team)

This may indicate that you are not a part of any team. Please contact support if you encounter this error

not\_in\_team

The user ID you are trying to query is not in your team.

require\_elevated\_privilege

The user does not have admin privileges to set the user role.

admin\_must\_exist

The team must have at least one admin. Please add an admin to the team or contact support if you encounter this error.

invalid\_args

An invalid argument was provided to the mutation for the `role` field. Please check the arguments you are providing and try again.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/set-user-role#additional-resources)

Additional Resources
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----\
\
Querying list of users](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/users)
[User\
----\
\
Querying user details](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user)

# Update Meeting Privacy - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Mutation

Update Meeting Privacy

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($input: UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput!) { updateMeetingPrivacy(input: $input) { id title privacy } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"input": {
    				"id": "your_transcript_id",
    				"privacy": "teammates"
    			}
    		}
    	}'

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "updateMeetingPrivacy": {
          "id": "your_transcript_id",
          "title": "Meeting Title",
          "privacy": "teammates"
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `updateMeetingPrivacy` mutation allows for updating the privacy setting of a meeting transcript. This operation requires admin privileges within the team or ownership of the meeting.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#arguments)

Arguments
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#param-input)

input

UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput

required

The privacy setting to be assigned to the meeting / transcript. See [UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-privacy-input)
.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#usage-example)

Usage Example
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To update a meeting’s privacy setting, provide the transcript ID and the new privacy level as arguments to the mutation. Here’s an example of how this mutation could be used:

Copy

Ask AI

    mutation UpdateMeetingPrivacy($input: UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput!) {
      updateMeetingPrivacy(input: $input) {
        id
        title
        privacy
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	-d '{
    		"query": "mutation($input: UpdateMeetingPrivacyInput!) { updateMeetingPrivacy(input: $input) { id title privacy } }",
    		"variables": {
    			"input": {
    				"id": "your_transcript_id",
    				"privacy": "teammates"
    			}
    		}
    	}'
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "updateMeetingPrivacy": {
          "id": "your_transcript_id",
          "title": "Meeting Title",
          "privacy": "teammates"
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#faq)

FAQ
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Who has permission to update meeting privacy?

Only users with admin privileges or meeting owners can update meeting privacy settings. The meeting owner also needs to be in your team.

What privacy levels are available?

Available privacy levels are: link (anyone with link), owner (meeting owner only), participants (meeting participants only), teammatesandparticipants (teammates and participants), teammates (teammates only).

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#error-codes)

Error Codes
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `updateMeetingPrivacy` mutation. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

require\_elevated\_privilege

The user must be either the meeting owner or a team admin to update meeting privacy.

object\_not\_found (transcript)

The specified transcript could not be found or you do not have access to it

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-privacy#additional-resources)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

--------------------\
\
Use the API to update meeting titles](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/mutation/update-meeting-title)

# Analytics query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Query

Analytics

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query Analytics($startTime: String, $endTime: String) { analytics(start_time: $startTime, end_time: $endTime) { team { conversation { average_filler_words } } } }", "variables": { "startTime": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z", "endTime": "2024-01-31T23:59:59Z" } }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "analytics": {
          "team": {
            "conversation": {
              "average_filler_words": 15
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The analytics query fetches detailed conversation and meeting metrics for teams and users across a specified date range.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#arguments)

Arguments
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#param-start-time)

start\_time

String

The `start_time` parameter filters results starting from a specific datetime (ISO 8601 format).

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#param-end-time)

end\_time

String

The `end_time` parameter filters results up to a specific datetime (ISO 8601 format).

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#schema)

Schema
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [Analytics](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/analytics)
 query.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#usage-example)

Usage Example
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query Analytics($startTime: String, $endTime: String) {
      analytics(start_time: $startTime, end_time: $endTime) {
        team {
          conversation {
            average_filler_words
            average_filler_words_diff_pct
            average_monologues_count
            average_monologues_count_diff_pct
            average_questions
            average_questions_diff_pct
            average_sentiments {
              negative_pct
              neutral_pct
              positive_pct
            }
            average_silence_duration
            average_silence_duration_diff_pct
            average_talk_listen_ratio
            average_words_per_minute
            longest_monologue_duration_sec
            longest_monologue_duration_diff_pct
            total_filler_words
            total_filler_words_diff_pct
            total_meeting_notes_count
            total_meetings_count
            total_monologues_count
            total_monologues_diff_pct
            teammates_count
            total_questions
            total_questions_diff_pct
            total_silence_duration
            total_silence_duration_diff_pct
          }
          meeting {
            count
            count_diff_pct
            duration
            duration_diff_pct
            average_count
            average_count_diff_pct
            average_duration
            average_duration_diff_pct
          }
        }
        users {
          user_id
          user_name
          user_email
          conversation {
            talk_listen_pct
            talk_listen_ratio
            total_silence_duration
            total_silence_duration_compare_to
            total_silence_pct
            total_silence_ratio
            total_speak_duration
            total_speak_duration_with_user
            total_word_count
            user_filler_words
            user_filler_words_compare_to
            user_filler_words_diff_pct
            user_longest_monologue_sec
            user_longest_monologue_compare_to
            user_longest_monologue_diff_pct
            user_monologues_count
            user_monologues_count_compare_to
            user_monologues_count_diff_pct
            user_questions
            user_questions_compare_to
            user_questions_diff_pct
            user_speak_duration
            user_word_count
            user_words_per_minute
            user_words_per_minute_compare_to
            user_words_per_minute_diff_pct
          }
          meeting {
            count
            count_diff
            count_diff_compared_to
            count_diff_pct
            duration
            duration_diff
            duration_diff_compared_to
            duration_diff_pct
          }
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
        -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
        -H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
        --data '{ "query": "query Analytics($startTime: String, $endTime: String) { analytics(start_time: $startTime, end_time: $endTime) { team { conversation { average_filler_words } } } }", "variables": { "startTime": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z", "endTime": "2024-01-31T23:59:59Z" } }' \
        https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "analytics": {
          "team": {
            "conversation": {
              "average_filler_words": 15
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#error-codes)

Error Codes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `analytics` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

paid\_required (business\_or\_higher)

You need to be on a Business or higher plan to query analytics.

require\_elevated\_privilege

The user does not have admin privileges to view analytics for team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/analytics#additional-resources)

# User query - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

Search...

Search...

Navigation

Query

User

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query User($userId: String!) { user(id: $userId) { name integrations } }", "variables": { "userId": "your_user_id" } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql

Response

Copy

Ask AI

{
      "data": {
        "user": {
          "name": "Justin Fly",
          "integrations": ["string"],
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

The user query is designed to fetch details associated with a specific user id.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#arguments)

Arguments
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#param-id)

id

String

`id` is an optional argument. Not passing an ID to this query will return user details for the owner of the API key

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#schema)

Schema
----------------------------------------------------------------------

Fields available to the [User](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/user)
 query

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#usage-example)

Usage Example
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query User($userId: String!) {
      user(id: $userId) {
        user_id
        recent_transcript
        recent_meeting
        num_transcripts
        name
        minutes_consumed
        is_admin
        integrations
        email
        user_groups {
          id
          name
          handle
          members {
            user_id
            first_name
            last_name
            email
          }
        }
      }
    }
    

curl

javascript

python

java

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X POST \
    	-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    	-H "Authorization: Bearer your_api_key" \
    	--data '{ "query": "query User($userId: String!) { user(id: $userId) { name integrations } }", "variables": { "userId": "your_user_id" } }' \
    	https://api.fireflies.ai/graphql
    

Response

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "user": {
          "name": "Justin Fly",
          "integrations": ["string"],
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#error-codes)

Error Codes
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

List of possible error codes that may be returned by the `user` query. Full list of error codes can be found [here](https://docs.fireflies.ai/miscellaneous/error-codes)
.

object\_not\_found (user)

The user ID you are trying to query does not exist.

not\_in\_team

The user ID you are trying to query is not in your team.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/graphql-api/query/user#additional-resources)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# UpdateMeetingTitleInput Schema - Fireflies.ai API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-title-input#content-area)

[Fireflies home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=89d57b6f64984918e600fab4b327d867)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/firefliesai/1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=1yZ69Sj9FG7Gc0Ag&q=85&s=46855320026ba559f9e81763bda4d1eb)](https://fireflies.ai/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Input

UpdateMeetingTitleInput

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-title-input#param-title)

title

String

required

The new title to be assigned to the meeting / transcript. The title must be a string between 5 and 250 characters long and should not contain any special characters.Min / max of 5 / 256 characters.

[​](https://docs.fireflies.ai/schema/input/update-meeting-title-input#param-id)

id

String

required

The unique identifier of the meeting / transcript.
